\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Self-\/define arrays for M\+E\+LA. 

\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
The first dimension (of size \mbox{[}T\+M\+C\+F\+M\+::n\+Supported\+Higgses=2\mbox{]}) supports a second resonance present in M\+C\+FM 
\end{DoxyAttention}
